The EXIF Date is important when uploading to the web especially one of the many cloud based photo storage services.\r\n\r\nThis application let you change the date and time different ways.\r\n\r\n1) You can set all dates and times to be the same (if you want) or just change the date and leave the time as they are.\r\n\r\n2) You can also use the Date Maths feature which lets you Add or Subtract Days, Months, Years, Hours, Minutes and/or Seconds from the current photo dates.\r\n\r\n3) You can sync all the dates to either the Creation, Modification or EXIF Date.\r\n\r\n4) You can also change each photo date and time individually.\r\n\r\nThe choice is really yours to make depending on the situation.\r\n\r\nBatch JPEG Date Changer requires a two-step process which firstly let you review the changes to the dates before applying them. So as not to make yet another boo boo which could ruin the day. Once you are happy with the changes, click the Change Now button and let the application do its magic.\r\n\r\nThe images will not be modified in any ways, it is only the file creation, modification dates and times will be changed.
